## Introduction 

This repository was created with the intention of helping developers master their concepts in JavaScript. It is not a requirement, but a guide for future studies. It is based on an article written by Stephen Curtis and you can read it [here](https://medium.com/@stephenthecurt/33-fundamentals-every-javascript-developer-should-know-13dd720a90d1).

**üöÄ Considered by GitHub as one of the [top open source projects of 2018!](https://blog.github.com/2018-12-13-new-open-source-projects/)**

## Community

Feel free to submit a PR adding a link to your own recaps or reviews. If you want to translate the repo into your native language, please feel free to do so.

32. **[‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤∂‡≤É ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç, ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤™‡≥ç](#32-‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤∂‡≤É-‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å-‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç-‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å-‡≤™‡≥à‡≤™‡≥ç)**
33. **[‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥Ä‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç](#33-‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥Ä‡≤®‡≥ç-‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç)**

- [‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≥Ä‡≤® ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‚Äî JavaScript.info](https://javascript.info/object-toprimitive)

## 4. Implicit, Explicit, Nominal, Structuring and Duck Typing

### <img  align= center width=40px height=40px src="https://cdn-icons-png.flaticon.com/512/1945/1945940.png"> Articles

-[‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤® ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¶‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‚Äî ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ö‡≤ø](https://dev.to/promhize/what-you-need-to-know-about-javascripts-implicit-coercion-e23)
- [‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤¶ ‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü - ‡≤Ö‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥ã‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç](https://medium.freecodecamp.org/js-type-coercion-explained-27ba3d9a2839)

## 7. Expression vs Statement

## 13. DOM and Layout Trees

### Books

### ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
